WBS Cellular Automata app generates patterns according to rules specified by the user. Sometimes very simple rules generate patterns of astonishing complexity. The patterns are generated on a two-dimensional lattice of cells. Each cell can be in one of two states: alive (on) or dead (off). A transition between the states is influenced by the cell’s neighbourhood – the eight cells surrounding the one in question.\r\n\r\nInitially, the lattice is populated randomly with alive and dead cells. After starting the simulation, the cells evolve by reproducing, dying, or surviving according to the user-defined rules. These rules are applied simultaneously to all the cells on the lattice.
